Interruptions ^nb1HQazD

guarantees visibility of writes between threads

Volatile ^HlakniOW

- changes are immediately visible to all threads
- established relationships between reads and writes -> all writes before volatile write are visible after volatile read ^1isqmV4E

values aren't cached in CPU cache =>
we always read from main memory ^pOBgHcNY

Atomicity ^csVbVanx

Atomic Statement ^y7SmRQKj

executed completely or not at all ^kh48oCZS

cannot be interleaved with other operations ^gUCNJGmT

produces no visible side effects until complete ^6HAE5IUq

no race conditions possible within a single atomic operation ^V4a2RIgv

however we can still get memory consistency errors without
a proper happens-before relationship ^xvIVmQXD

reading / writing reference variables ^3cddZqjt

reading / writing most primitives ^AwRV6AXS

reading / writing volatile variables (also establishes
happens-before but doesn't lock) ^O2kIszdm
